Sets the constants for smoothing out a path.

Path smoothing based on \href{https://medium.com/@jaems33/understanding-robot-motion-path-smoothing-5970c8363bc4}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+medium.\+com/\+@jaems33/\+understanding-\/robot-\/motion-\/path-\/smoothing-\/5970c8363bc4}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em weight\+\_\+smooth} & how much weight to update the data \\
\hline
{\em weight\+\_\+data} & how much weight to smooth the coordinates \\
\hline
{\em tolerance} & how much change per iteration is necessary to keep iterating \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
